deepCopyMap(settings)\n   325→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(result)\n   326→\n   327→\tfor _, config := range configs {\n   328→\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n   329→\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) && v != 333→\t\t\t\t}\n   334→\n   335→\t\t\t\tencryptedSecret, err := s.secrets.Encrypt(ctx, []byte(strValue), secrets.WithoutScope())\n   336→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   337→\t\t\t\t\treturn result, err\n   338→\t\t\t\t}\n   339→\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = base64.RawStdEncoding.EncodeToString(encryptedSecret)\n   340→\t\t\t}\n   341→\t\t}\n   342→\t}\n   343→\n   344→\treturn result, nil\n   345→}\n   346→\n   347→func (s *Service) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n   348→\tinterval := s.cfg.SSOSettingsReloadInterval\n   349→\tif interval == 0 {\n   350→\t\treturn nil\n   351→\t}\n   352→\n   353→\tticker := time.NewTicker(interval)\n   354→\n   355→\t// start a background process for reloading the SSO settings for all providers at a fixed interval\n   356→\t// it is useful for high availability setups running multiple Grafana instances\n   357→\tfor {\n   358→\t\tselect {\n   359→\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n   360→\t\t\ts.doReload(ctx)\n   361→\n   362→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   363→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   364→\t\t}\n   365→\t}\n   366→}\n   367→\n   368→func (s *Service) doReload(ctx context.Context) {\n   369→\ts.logger.Debug(\"reloading SSO Settings for all providers\")\n   370→\n   371→\tsettingsList, err := s.List(ctx)\n   372→\tif err != nil {\n   373→\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to fetch SSO Settings for all providers\", \"err\", err)\n   374→\t\treturn\n   375→\t}\n   376→\n   377→\tfor provider, connector := range s.reloadables {\n   378→\t\tsettings := getSettingByProvider(provider, settingsList)\n   379→\n   380→\t\tif settings == nil || len(settings.Settings) == 0 {\n   381→\t\t\ts.logger.Warn(\"SSO Settings is empty\", \"provider\", provider)\n   382→\t\t\tcontinue\n   383→\t\t}\n   384→\n   385→\t\terr = connector.Reload(ctx, *settings)\n   386→\t\tif err != nil {\n   387→\t\t\ts.metrics.reloadFailures.WithLabelValues(provider).Inc()\n   388→\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to reload SSO Settings\", \"provider\", provider, \"err\", err)\n   389→\t\t\tcontinue\n   390→\t\t}\n   391→\t}\n   392→}\n   393→\n   394→// mergeSSOSettings merges the settings from the database with the system settings\n   395→// Required because it is possible that the user has configured some of the settings (current Advanced OAuth settings)\n   396→// and the rest of the settings have to be loaded from the system settings\n   397→func (s *Service) mergeSSOSettings(dbSettings, systemSettings *models.SSOSettings) *models.SSOSettings {\n   398→\tif dbSettings == nil {\n   399→\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"No SSO Settings found in the database, using system settings\")\n   400→\t\treturn systemSettings\n   401→\t}\n   402→\n   403→\ts.logger.Debug(\"Merging SSO Settings\", \"dbSettings\", removeSecrets(dbSettings.Settings), \"systemSettings\", removeSecrets(systemSettings.Settings))\n   404→\n   405→\tresult := &models.SSOSettings{\n   406→\t\tProvider: dbSettings.Provider,\n   407→\t\tSource:   dbSettings.Source,\n   408→\t\tSettings: mergeSettings(dbSettings.Settings, systemSettings.Settings),\n   409→\t\tCreated:  dbSettings.Created,\n   410→\t\tUpdated:  dbSettings.Updated,\n   411→\t}\n   412→\n   413→\treturn result\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→func (s *Service) decryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   417→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(settings)\n   418→\n   419→\tfor _, dbSettings.Source,\n\t\tSettings: mergeSettings(dbSettings.Settings, systemSettings.Settings),\n\t\tCreated:  dbSettings.Created,\n\t\tUpdated:  dbSettings.Updated,\n\t}\n\n\treturn result\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) decryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(settings)\n\n\tfor _, config := range configs {\n\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) && v != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to parse secret value, it is not a string\", \"key\", k)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tdecoded, err := base64.RawStdEncoding.DecodeString(strValue)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to decode secret string\", \"err\", err, \"value\")\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tdecrypted, err := s.secrets.Decrypt(ctx, decoded)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to decrypt secret\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = string(decrypted)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn settings, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) isProviderConfigurable(provider string) bool {\n\tenabled, ok := s.configurableProviders[provider]\n\treturn ok && enabled\n}\n\n// removeSecrets removes all the secrets from the map and replaces them with a redacted password\n// and returns a new map\nfunc removeSecrets(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tresult := deepCopyMap(settings)\n\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(result)\n\n\tfor _, config := range configs {\n\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n\t\t\tval, ok := v.(string)\n\t\t\tif ok && val != \"\" && IsSecretField(k) {\n\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = setting.RedactedPassword\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// getConfigMaps returns a list of maps that may contain secrets\nfunc getConfigMaps(settings map[string]any) []map[string]any {\n\t// always include the main settings map\n\tresult := []map[string]any{settings}\n\n\t// for LDAP include settings for each server\n\tif config, ok := settings[\"config\"].(map[string]any); ok {\n\t\tif servers, ok := config[\"servers\"].([]any); ok {\n\t\t\tfor _, server := range servers {\n\t\t\t\tif serverSettings, ok := server.(map[string]any); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tresult = append(result, serverSettings)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// mergeSettings merges two maps in a way that the values from the first map are preserved\n// and the values from the second map are added only if they don't exist in the first map\n// or if they contain empty URLs.\nfunc mergeSettings(storedSettings, systemSettings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tsettings := make(map[string]any)\n\n\tfor k, v := range storedSettings {\n\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t}\n\n\tfor k, v := range systemSettings {\n\t\tif _, ok := settings[k]; !ok {\n\t\t\tif isMergingAllowed(k) {\n\t\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if isURL(k) && isEmptyString(settings[k]) {\n\t\t\t// Overwrite all URL settings from the DB containing an empty string with their value\n\t\t\t// from the system settings. This fixes an issue with empty auth_url, api_url and token_url\n\t\t\t// from the DB not being replaced with their values defined in the system settings for\n\t\t\t// the Google provider.\n\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn settings\n}\n\n// isMergingAllowed returns true if the field provided can be merged from the system settings.\n// It won't allow SAML fields that are part of a group of settings to be merged from system settings\n// because the DB settings already contain one valid setting from each group.\nfunc isMergingAllowed(fieldName string) bool {\n\tforbiddenMergePatterns := []string{\"certificate\", \"private_key\", \"idp_metadata\"}\n\n\tfor _, v := range forbiddenMergePatterns {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// mergeSecrets returns a new map with the current value for secrets that have not been updated\nfunc mergeSecrets(settings map[string]any, storedSettings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n\tsettingsWithSecrets := deepCopyMap(settings)\n\tnewConfigs := getConfigMaps(settingsWithSecrets)\n\tstoredConfigs := getConfigMaps(storedSettings)\n\n\tfor i, config := range newConfigs {\n\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) {\n\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif !isNewSecretValue(strValue) && len(storedConfigs) > i {\n\t\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = storedConfigs[i][k] // use the currently stored value\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn settingsWithSecrets, nil\n}\n\nfunc overrideMaps(maps ...map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tresult := make(map[string]any)\n\tfor _, m := range maps {\n\t\tfor k, v := range m {\n\t\t\tresult[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// IsSecretField returns true if the SSO settings field provided is a secret\nfunc IsSecretField(fieldName string) bool {\n\tsecretFieldPatterns := []string{\"secret\", \"private\", \"certificate\", \"password\", \"client_key\"}\n\n\tfor _, v := range secretFieldPatterns {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc isURL(fieldName string) bool {\n\treturn strings.HasSuffix(fieldName, \"_url\")\n}\n\nfunc isEmptyString(val any) bool {\n\t_, ok := val.(string)\n\treturn ok && val == \"\"\n}\n\nfunc isNewSecretValue(value string) bool {\n\treturn value != setting.RedactedPassword\n}\n\nfunc deepCopyMap(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tnewSettings := make(map[string]any)\n\n\tfor key, value := range settings {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[string]any:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopyMap(v)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopySlice(v)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = value\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn newSettings\n}\n\nfunc deepCopySlice(s []any) []any {\n\tnewSlice := make([]any, len(s))\n\n\tfor i, value := range s {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[string]any:\n\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = deepCopyMap(v)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = deepCopySlice(v)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = value\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn newSlice\n}\n","numLines":622,"startLine":1,"totalLines":622}}}

/api/v1/sso-settings/:key`: Get specific provider settings (read permission per provider scope)\\n  - `PUT /api/v1/sso-settings/:key`: Update provider settings (write permission per provider scope)\\n
